        Long_term_interest_rate_used_by_private_lenders[us] * GDP_USED[us]/ Global_GDP_USED
        + Long_term_interest_rate_used_by_private_lenders[cn] * GDP_USED[cn] / Global_GDP_USED
        + Long_term_interest_rate_used_by_private_lenders[af] * GDP_USED[af] / Global_GDP_USED
        + Long_term_interest_rate_used_by_private_lenders[me] * GDP_USED[me] / Global_GDP_USED
        + Long_term_interest_rate_used_by_private_lenders[pa] * GDP_USED[pa] / Global_GDP_USED
        + Long_term_interest_rate_used_by_private_lenders[ec] * GDP_USED[ec] / Global_GDP_USED
        + Long_term_interest_rate_used_by_private_lenders[eu] * GDP_USED[eu] / Global_GDP_USED
        + Long_term_interest_rate_used_by_private_lenders[la] * GDP_USED[la] / Global_GDP_USED
        + Long_term_interest_rate_used_by_private_lenders[sa] * GDP_USED[sa] / Global_GDP_USED
        + Long_term_interest_rate_used_by_private_lenders[se] * GDP_USED[se] / Global_GDP_USED
